The disadvantages are that the carpet in the elevator corridor out of the floor is stained, and slippers are placed in the bedside table in the room (a common appearance in farmhouses). Obviously, the room is large and has a lot of space and even a separate cloakroom for storage. Why put slippers in the bedside table? The view is ugly and the smell is unpleasant. There is no heating during the day. It is cold in winter at about 5 degrees. The heating will not start until 6 or 7 o'clock in the evening. Breakfast is OK, with freshly ground coffee. But the male chef who cooks rice noodles for breakfast seems to be in a particularly bad mood. He doesn't say a word to anyone and has a bad face. No one conflicts with him, which is strange. This hotel is generally cost-effective!
